### [1] [Scale-Gest: Scalable Model-Space Synthesis and Runtime Selection for On-Device Gesture Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12506)
*Abdul Basit,Saim Rehman,Muhammad Shafique*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Scale-Gest：在设备端以运行时自适应方式进行手势检测，通过在tiny-YOLO家族内扩展多尺度模型与分辨率/步幅配置，并结合电池/用户约束的控制器与ROI裁剪，以保持事件级F1不降同时显著降低能耗与时延。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在移动/电池供电设备上做ML手势检测受实时、能耗、内存限制，且电量水平变化导致固定单模型难以在准确度与资源之间最优权衡；需要能随设备与任务约束动态权衡的自适应框架。

Method: 1) 扩展检测器空间为密集的tiny-YOLO架构族，跨模型-分辨率-步幅形成运行点；2) 通过设备校准得到ACE(准确度-复杂度-能耗)剖面；3) 设计轻量运行时控制器，依据用户与电池约束选择ACE模式；4) 引入运动感知的手部ROI门控以裁剪输入，降低计算；5) 构建并用车载驾驶场景的DSG-18时序标注数据集评估。

Result: 在电池供电笔记本的手势流上，相比单一检测器，ACE控制器将帧级能耗从6.9 mJ降至1.6 mJ（约4倍降低），在保持事件级F1=0.8–0.9与低平均时延6 ms的同时实现能耗与延迟显著下降。

Conclusion: 运行时自适应、多尺度tiny-YOLO与设备校准ACE剖面结合ROI门控，可在不牺牲事件级准确度的前提下显著降低设备端手势检测的能耗与延迟；适用于电池受限与动态约束的边缘AI场景。

Abstract: Realizing on-device ML-based gesture detection under tight real-time performance, energy and memory constraints is challenging, especially when considering mobile devices with varying battery-power levels. Existing EdgeAI deployments typically rely on a single fixed detector, limiting optimization opportunities. We present Scale-Gest, a novel run-time adaptive gesture detection framework that expands the detector space into a dense family of tiny-YOLO architectures. We introduce multiple novel device-calibrated ACE (Accuracy-Complexity-Energy) profiles by analyzing different model-resolution-stride operating points. A lightweight run-time controller selects an appropriate ACE mode under user-defined and battery constraints, while a motion-aware hand-gesture-tracking ROI gate crops the input for reduced complexity detection. To evaluate performance of our system in real-world car driving scenarios, we introduce a temporally-annotated Driver Simulated Gesture (DSG-18) dataset. Scale-Gest maintains event-level F1 while significantly reducing energy and latency compared to single-detector approaches. On a battery-powered laptop running gesture streams, our ACE controller reduces per-frame energy by 4x (from 6.9 mJ to 1.6 mJ) while maintaining high gesture-detection performance (event-level F1 = 0.8-0.9) and low mean latency (6 ms).

</details>


### [2] [MorphOPC: Advancing Mask Optimization with Multi-scale Hierarchical Morphological Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12528)
*Yuting Hu,Lei Zhuang,Chen Wang,Ruiyang Qin,Hua Xiang,Gi-joon Nam,Jinjun Xiong*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出MorphOPC：以形态学操作为核心的多尺度层级模型，显著提升OPC/ILT中的掩模生成质量与成本效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于编码器-解码器的生成式掩模优化模型难以精准学习从目标版图到掩模图形的几何变换，导致打印保真度与可制造性不足。随着工艺进入纳米尺度，这一问题更为突出，需要能直接表达形态学几何变换的学习框架。

Method: 将掩模生成建模为局部版图特征上一系列形态学（膨胀/腐蚀/开闭等）操作的序列；设计多尺度层级结构，内含可微的神经形态学模块，用以学习并组合这些操作；在金属与通孔层的边缘型OPC与ILT基准上进行训练与评测。

Result: 在多个基准上，MorphOPC相较SOTA方法取得更高的打印保真度与更低的制造成本，表现稳定且可扩展。

Conclusion: 形态学先验与多尺度层级设计能有效捕捉从目标版图到掩模图形的几何变换，MorphOPC为可扩展、高质量的掩模优化提供了有力方案。

Abstract: As feature sizes shrink to the nanometer scale, accurately transferring circuit patterns from photomasks to silicon wafers becomes increasingly challenging. Optical proximity correction (OPC) is widely used to ensure pattern fidelity and manufacturability. Recent generative mask optimization models based on encoder-decoder architecture can synthesize near-optimal masks, serving as fast machine learning (ML) surrogates for traditional OPC. However, these models often fail to capture the geometric transformations from target layouts to mask patterns, leading to suboptimal quality. In this work, we formulate mask generation as a sequence of morphological operations on local layout features and propose \textit{MorphOPC}, a multi-scale hierarchical model with neural morphological modules to learn these transformations. Experiments on edge-based OPC and ILT benchmarks across metal and via layers show that \textit{MorphOPC} consistently outperforms state-of-the-art methods, achieving higher printing fidelity and lower manufacturing cost, demonstrating strong potential for scalable mask optimization.

</details>


### [3] [CROP: Expert-Aligned Image Cropping via Compositional Reasoning and Optimizing Preference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12545)
*Zhitong Dong,Chao Li,Jie Yu,Hao Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出将审美裁剪视为多模态推理任务，设计CROP框架，通过“分析-提案-决策”链式思考与专家偏好对齐，使裁剪结果更贴近人类专业水准，并在多数据集上优于既有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖显著性或检索相似案例，缺乏对构图与审美的深层理解：显著性难以在复杂场景中做取舍，检索方法缺少对独特场景的自适应推理，导致与专家裁剪不一致。

Method: 将审美裁剪重新表述为多模态推理任务，提出CROP：引导VLM像专业摄影师那样进行“分析-提案-决策”的逐步推理，围绕场景要素与构图原则分解问题；并加入专家偏好对齐模块，使模型决策与人类专家审美一致。

Result: 在多个数据集上进行大量实验，方法整体性能优于现有方案，并通过消融验证各组件有效。

Conclusion: 通过多模态链式推理与专家偏好对齐，CROP更好地处理复杂主观的审美裁剪问题，使自动裁剪结果更贴近人类专家判断并在基准上取得领先。

Abstract: Aesthetic image cropping aims to enhance the aesthetic quality of an image by improving its composition through spatial cropping. Previous methods often rely on saliency prediction or retrieval augmentation, ignoring the task's core requirement: a deep understanding of composition and aesthetics. Consequently, saliency-based methods struggle to make compositional trade-offs in complex scenes, while retrieval-based methods blindly refer to similar cases, lacking adaptive reasoning for unique scenes. Both approaches fail to align their automated cropping results with those of human experts. To address the above issues, we propose a novel paradigm that reformulates aesthetic cropping as a multimodal reasoning task, aiming to activate the VLM's analytical and comprehension capabilities in aesthetics. We design a Compositional Reasoning and Optimizing Preference method (CROP) that directs the VLM to think like a professional photographer. It deconstructs a complex and subjective aesthetic problem into an "analysis-proposal-decision" process, reasoning step by step through the analysis of scene elements and compositional principles. Meanwhile, our expert preference alignment module makes the model's decision consistent with human expert aesthetics. Extensive experiments across multiple datasets validate our method's superiority and component effectiveness.

</details>


### [4] [What Happens Before Decoding? Prefill Determines GUI Grounding in VLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12549)
*Jiaping Lin,Fei Shen,Junzhe Li,Ping Nie,Fei Yu,Ming Li,Haizhou Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Re-Prefill：一种无需训练的GUI定位方法，通过在推理时增加“注意力引导的第二次prefill”来提升候选UI元素选择，从而显著提高坐标定位准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有无需训练的GUI grounding方法常依赖多次前向推理（迭代裁剪/候选聚合），但每次前向仍独立理解指令与版面，缺少跨视觉token的渐进交互。作者通过分析VLM的推理流程，发现grounding存在关键瓶颈：prefill阶段决定候选元素，一旦候选选错，解码阶段难以纠正。

Method: 提出Re-Prefill：1）观察到最终token对视觉token的跨层注意力可暴露潜在目标；2）在第一次prefill后，提取在多层中持续获得高注意力的视觉token，形成初步目标假设；3）将这些高注意力视觉token与指令的隐状态一并“回灌”到模型输入，执行第二次attention-guided prefill，让模型在生成坐标前“重新思考”；全程无需额外训练。

Result: 在4个VLM、5个GUI基准（ScreenSpot-Pro、ScreenSpot-V2、OSWorld-G、UI-Vision、MMBench-GUI）上，一致提升，ScreenSpot-Pro上最高提升4.3%。

Conclusion: GUI grounding存在“prefill定候选、解码做微调”的两阶段不对称性，prefill是性能瓶颈。通过Re-Prefill在推理期强化候选选择，可在无需训练的条件下稳定提升多模型多数据集的定位效果。

Abstract: Existing training-free approaches for GUI grounding often rely on multiple inference runs, such as iterative cropping or candidate aggregation, to identify target elements. Despite this additional computation, each forward pass still independently interprets the instruction and parses the visual layout, without enabling progressive interaction among visual tokens. In this paper, we study what happens during GUI grounding in Vision-Language Models (VLMs) and identify a previously overlooked bottleneck. We show that grounding follows a two-stage paradigm: the prefill stage determines candidate UI elements, while the decoding stage subsequently refines the final coordinates. This asymmetry establishes prefill as the critical step, as errors in candidate selection cannot be effectively corrected during decoding. Based on this observation, we propose Re-Prefill, a training-free method that revisits inference by introducing an attention-guided second prefill stage to refine target selection. Specifically, visual tokens that consistently receive high attention from the query position, i.e., the final token, across layers are extracted as a preliminary target hypothesis and appended to the input, together with the instruction hidden states, enabling the model to deeply re-think its decision before coordinate generation. Experiments across four VLMs and five benchmarks, including ScreenSpot-Pro, ScreenSpot-V2, OSWorld-G, UI-Vision, and MMBench-GUI, demonstrate consistent improvements without additional training, with gains of up to 4.3% on ScreenSpot-Pro. Code will be available at https://github.com/linjiaping1/Re-Prefill.

</details>


### [5] [SSDA: Bridging Spectral and Structural Gaps via Dual Adaptation for Vision-Based Time Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12550)
*Mingrui Zhang,Hanchen Yang,Wengen Li,Xudong Jiang,Yichao Zhang,Jihong Guan,Shuigeng Zhou*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文指出将时间序列渲染为图像交给大型视觉模型（LVM）进行预测虽有效，但存在“谱差异”和“结构差异”。为此提出SSDA：在数据层用SMA通过2D FFT调整幅度谱贴近自然图像、保留相位；在模型层用SG-LoRA注入时序位置编码并以低秩更新适配注意力；双分支自适应融合。多数据集上，SSDA在全样本与小样本均优于强基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前做法依赖“时间序列图像近似自然图像”这一未被充分检验的前提。作者发现：渲染后的时间序列图像的功率谱更平坦（与自然图像1/f规律不符）；把1D序列重排为2D网格会制造伪邻近、破坏真实时序相邻，导致预训练LVM的空间归纳偏置被误导。动机是显式弥合这两类差异以更好迁移LVM能力到时序预测。

Method: 提出SSDA双分支适配：1) 光谱分支SMA：对渲染图像做2D FFT，只调整幅度谱以向自然图像统计对齐，保持相位不变，从而保留结构信息同时校正频谱；2) 结构分支SG-LoRA：在补丁嵌入阶段注入基于时间位置的编码，并通过低秩适配（LoRA）微调注意力，使模型关注真实时间连续性而非伪2D邻近；3) 自适应融合两分支输出得到最终预测。

Result: 在7个真实世界基准上，SSDA在全量训练与小样本设置下都稳定优于强LVM与LLM基线（具体数值未在摘要给出），代码已开源。

Conclusion: LVM直接用于时间序列预测受限于频谱和结构错配。通过SMA的频谱对齐与SG-LoRA的结构感知适配，并进行分支融合，能显著提升跨模态迁移与预测性能。

Abstract: Large vision models (LVMs) have recently proven to be surprisingly effective time series forecasters, simply by rendering temporal data as images. This success, how ever, rests on a largely unexamined premise: the rendered time series images are sufficiently close to natural images for knowledge in pre-trained models to transfer effectively. We argue that two gaps still remain, i.e., spectral and structural gaps, fundamentally limiting the potential of LVMs for time series forecasting. Spectrally, we systematically reveal that rendered time series images exhibit a markedly shallower power spectrum than the natural images LVMs are pre-trained to recognize. Structurally, reshaping 1D temporal sequences into 2D grids fabricates spurious spatial adjacencies while severing genuine temporal continuities, misleading the spatial inductive biases of pre-trained LVMs. To bridge these gaps, we propose SSDA, a dual-branch network that spectrally and structurally adapts to unlock the full potential of LVMs for time series forecasting. At the data level, a Spectral Magnitude Aligner (SMA) applies 2D FFT to selectively enhance the magnitude spectrum toward natural-image statistics while preserving phase. At the model level, a Structural-Guided Low-Rank Adaptation (SG-LoRA) injects position-aware temporal encodings into patch embeddings and adapts at tention via low-rank updates. The two branches are further adaptively fused to produce the final forecast. Extensive experiments on seven real-world benchmarks demonstrate that SSDA consistently outperforms strong LVM- and LLM-based baselines under both full-shot and few-shot settings. Code is publicly available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/SSDA-8C5B.

</details>


### [6] [M2Retinexformer: Multi-Modal Retinexformer for Low-Light Image Enhancement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12556)
*Youssef Aboelwafa,Hicham G. Elmongui,Marwan Torki*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出M2Retinexformer：在Retinexformer基础上引入深度、亮度先验与语义特征的多模态渐进增强框架，通过跨注意力与自适应门控融合多尺度模态，在LOL、SID、SMID、SDSD上优于SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单一RGB信息难以应对低照度图像中的复合退化（噪声放大、伪影、色偏）；需要引入与光照不变或能提供先验的外部线索（深度、亮度分布、语义）以提升稳健性与泛化。

Method: 扩展Retinexformer为多模态结构：从深度、亮度先验与语义通道提取多尺度特征；设计跨注意力模块进行模态交互；引入自适应门控在“照明引导的自注意力”和“跨注意力”间动态加权，依据辅助模态可信度调整融合；采用渐进式细化管线逐步提升亮度与去噪、纠偏。

Result: 在LOL、SID、SMID、SDSD数据集上全面超过Retinexformer与近期SOTA，代码和预训练模型开源。

Conclusion: 多模态（深度、亮度先验、语义）与自适应跨注意力融合能显著提升低照度增强的稳健性与质量，证明了跨模态先验对Retinex范式的有效补充。

Abstract: Low-light image enhancement is challenging due to complex degradations, including amplified noise, artifacts, and color distortion. While Retinex-based deep learning methods have achieved promising results, they primarily rely on single-modality RGB information. We propose M2Retinexformer (Multi-Modal Retinexformer), a novel framework that extends Retinexformer by incorporating depth cues, luminance priors, and semantic features within a progressive refinement pipeline. Depth provides geometric context that is invariant to lighting variations, while luminance and semantic features offer explicit guidance on brightness distribution and scene understanding. Modalities are extracted at multiple scales and fused through cross-attention, with adaptive gating dynamically balancing illumination-guided self-attention and cross-attention based on the reliability of auxiliary cues. Evaluations on the LOL, SID, SMID, and SDSD benchmarks demonstrate overall improvements over Retinexformer and recent state-of-the-art methods. Code and pretrained weights are available at https://github.com/YoussefAboelwafa/M2Retinexformer

</details>


### [7] [Pyramid Self-contrastive Learning Framework for Test-time Ultrasound Image Denoising](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12567)
*Jiajing Zhang,Bingze Dai,Xi Zhang,Yue Xu,Wei-Ning Lee*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出A2A纯测试时训练框架，在合成孔径超声( SAU )上一枪式去噪，通过自对比学习在金字塔潜空间分离解剖与噪声，解码出清晰图像。无需预训练与先验噪声假设，显著提升SNR/CNR，体内外均验证有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统超声去噪方法要么依赖固定噪声模型、在复合噪声下失效，要么需要大量标注与预训练，且存在域移，导致泛化差与结构模糊。需要一种在复杂体内环境下、无需预训练、能适应多噪声且保留结构细节的方法。

Method: 在SAU中使用“孔到孔”(A2A)框架：对打乱的子孔径数据进行自对比学习，在多尺度（金字塔）潜空间中解耦“解剖相似性”(共享成分)与“噪声随机性”(非共享成分)；随后仅从解剖子空间解码出干净图像/信号并丢弃噪声子空间。训练发生在测试时、基于单个带噪样本（one-shot），无需预训练与外部数据。

Result: 仿真：在电子噪声0–30 dB与不同内含体几何下，SNR提升69.3%，CNR提升34.4%。体内：心脏六个超声切面、肝脏、肾脏，仅用两个孔径数据即可，SNR提升84.8%，CNR提升25.7%，在多目标与成像配置下均得到更清晰结果。

Conclusion: A2A在测试时以单样本自适应地分离解剖与噪声，避免域移与预训练成本，实现对复合噪声的鲁棒去噪并保留结构细节，为更可靠的超声解剖可视化与功能评估铺平道路。

Abstract: The inherent electronic and speckle noise complicates clinical interpretation of ultrasound images. Conventional denoising methods rely on explicit noise assumptions whose validity diminishes under composite noise conditions. Learning-based methods require massive labeled data and model parameters. These pre-defined and pre-trained manners entail an inevitable domain shift in complex in vivo environments, so they are limited to a specific noise type and often blur structural details. In this study, we propose a pure test-time training framework for one-shot ultrasound image denoising and apply it to synthetic aperture ultrasound (SAU), which synthesizes transmit focus from sub-aperture transmissions. Our Aperture-to-Aperture (A2A) framework disentangles anatomical similarity and noise randomness from shuffled sub-apertures through self-contrastive learning in pyramid latent spaces. The clean image is then decoded from the anatomy space, while discarding the noise space. A2A is trained at test time on one noisy sample of SAU signals, so it fundamentally eliminates the domain shift and pretraining costs. Simulation experiments, including electronic noise levels of 0 to 30 dB and different inclusion geometries, demonstrated an improvement of 69.3% SNR and 34.4% CNR by A2A. The in vivo results showed 84.8% SNR and 25.7% CNR gains using only two aperture data of the heart in six echocardiographic views, liver, and kidney. A2A delivers clear images/signals across diverse imaging targets and configurations, paving the way for more reliable anatomical visualization and functional assessment by ultrasound.

</details>


### [8] [M3Net: A Macro-to-Meso-to-Micro Clinical-inspired Hierarchical 3D Network for Pulmonary Nodule Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12570)
*Jinyue Li,Yuzhou Yu,Jingjing Yang,Meng Fu,Yani Zhang,Shuyao He,Dianlong Ge,Xin Ning,Yannan Chu,Qiankun Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出M3Net：受放射科分级诊断流程启发的3D多尺度肺结节良恶性分类网络，在LIDC-IDRI与USTC-FHLN上分别达86.96%与84.24%准确率，显著优于现有方法并具备更强可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有肺结节分类难点在于结节多尺度、形态异质导致的判别困难；深度模型虽有效但多为黑箱，缺乏跨尺度语义一致与可解释性，限制临床落地。

Method: 构建从精细结节结构→局部语义→全局解剖关系的渐进式多尺度输入；为各尺度设计专属编码器；通过潜在空间投影与互信息最大化实现跨尺度语义一致；整体为3D网络框架（M3Net），对多尺度上下文进行融合并增强可解释性。

Result: 在公开LIDC-IDRI与自建USTC-FHLN数据集上取得SOTA：准确率分别为86.96%与84.24%，相较最佳基线提升3.26%与2.17%，表现稳健。

Conclusion: M3Net有效整合多尺度上下文并通过语义一致性约束提升可解释性与鲁棒性，为临床可用的肺结节分类提供更可信方案；代码开源，便于复现与扩展。

Abstract: The accurate classification of benign and malignant pulmonary nodules in CT scans is critical for early lung cancer screening, yet remains challenging due to the multi-scale and heterogeneous nature of pulmonary nodules. While deep learning offers potential for auxiliary diagnosis, most existing models act as "black boxes", lacking the transparency and explainability required for trustworthy clinical integration. To address this issue, we propose M3Net, a novel 3D network for pulmonary nodule classification inspired by the hierarchical diagnostic workflow of radiologists, which integrates multi-scale contextual information from fine-grained structures to global anatomical relationships. Our framework constructs a progressive multi-scale input, from fine-grained nodule structures to local semantics and global spatial relationships. M3Net employs scale-specific encoders and ensures cross-scale semantic consistency through latent space projection and mutual information maximization. Extensive experiments on the public LIDC-IDRI dataset and a self-collected clinical dataset (USTC-FHLN) demonstrate that our method achieves state-of-the-art performance, with accuracies of 86.96% and 84.24% respectively, outperforming the best baseline by 3.26% and 2.17%. The results validate that M3Net provides a more robust and clinically relevant solution for pulmonary nodule classification. The code is available at https://github.com/jylEcho/M3-Net.

</details>


### [9] [VideoSEAL: Mitigating Evidence Misalignment in Agentic Long Video Understanding by Decoupling Answer Authority](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12571)
*Chenhao Qiu,Yechao Zhang,Xin Luo,Shien Song,Xusheng Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出解耦式“规划—核验”框架来解决长视频问答中的证据错配问题，在多个基准上同时提升正确率与证据对齐度，并能随搜索预算与骨干模型升级而稳健扩展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态大模型在短视频问答表现尚可，但在长视频中需要跨长时间跨度搜索稀疏证据并进行多轮核验。现有长视频智能体常出现“证据错配”：答案虽然正确，但与检索/查看到的证据不一致。作者希望诊断与缓解这类失配，提升答案与像素级证据的一致性与可解释性。

Method: 1) 提出两项诊断指标：时间扎根性（是否在正确时间段取证）与语义扎根性（检索段落是否语义支撑答案）。2) 分析两种导致错配的压力：推理时共享上下文饱和造成的提示压力、训练时仅结果导向带来的奖励压力。3) 提出结构性解决方案：解耦式“规划—核验”框架（decoupled planner-inspector）。规划器负责长程检索与搜索轨迹；检验器拥有最终答复权限，必须进行像素级核验后才给出答案。该架构支持可解释搜索、可扩展搜索预算，并可即插即用替换/升级MLLM骨干而无需重训规划器。

Result: 在四个长视频基准上同时提升答案准确率与证据对齐：LVBench 55.1%，LongVideoBench 62.0%，并展示出可解释的搜索轨迹与随预算稳健扩展的性能；支持在不重训规划器的情况下更换更强的MLLM骨干。

Conclusion: 长视频问答中的证据错配源于将长程规划与答案权威耦合的结构性问题。通过将规划与核验解耦，并用像素级核验把关，既能提高准确率，又能确保证据对齐和可解释性，同时具备良好扩展性与模块化升级能力。

Abstract: Long video question answering requires locating sparse, time-scattered visual evidence within highly redundant content. Although current MLLMs perform well on short videos, long videos introduce long-horizon search and verification, which often necessitates multi-turn, agentic interaction. We show that existing LVU agents can exhibit "evidence misalignment": they produce correct answers that are not supported by the retrieved or inspected evidence. To characterize this failure, we introduce two diagnostics (temporal groundedness and semantic groundedness) and use them to reveal two pressures that amplify misalignment: prompt pressure from shared-context saturation at inference time and reward pressure from outcome-only optimization during training. These findings point to a structural root cause: the coupled agent paradigm conflates long-horizon planning with answer authority. We therefore propose the decoupled planner-inspector framework, which separates planning from answer authority and gates final answering on pixel-level verification. Across four long-video benchmarks, our framework improves both answer accuracy and evidence alignment, achieving 55.1% on LVBench and 62.0% on LongVideoBench while producing interpretable search trajectories. Moreover, the decoupled architecture scales consistently with increased search budgets and supports plug-and-play upgrades of the MLLM backbone without retraining the planner. Code and models are available at https://github.com/Echochef/VideoSEAL.

### [10] [Improving Diffusion Posterior Samplers with Lagged Temporal Corrections for Image Restoration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12573)
*Davide Evangelista,Elena Morotti,Francesco Pivi,Maurizio Gabbrielli*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出LAMP：在扩散式后验采样(PS)框架中引入二阶离散与残差校正的模块化插件，不增推理步数即可在多种成像逆问题上优于DiffPIR与DDRM。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统PS依赖“瞬时”数据一致性估计，导致反向动力学随时间波动；缺乏对时间变化的系统建模，可能限制采样质量与稳定性。

Method: 将PS重释为离散化的扩散动力系统：标准PS=一阶离散+“去噪预测-数据一致估计”之间的残差校正。提出在此基础上加入二阶离散引出的时间项（利用相邻估计的变化），并与残差校正结合，形成带“滞后”时间修正的LAMP；以插件方式叠加在任意PS骨干上，并给出一步风险分析以刻画偏差-方差权衡与改进条件。

Result: 在多种成像任务中，相比DiffPIR、DDRM等强基线，LAMP在不增加去噪评估次数的前提下取得一致提升。

Conclusion: 二阶时间校正与残差校正的结合可稳健改善扩散PS的逆向过渡，保持后验采样结构，并在计算成本不变的情况下带来性能提升。

Abstract: Diffusion-based posterior sampling (PS) is a leading framework for imaging inverse problems, combining learned priors with measurement constraints. Yet, its standard formulations rely on instantaneous data-consistent estimates, which induce temporal variability in the reverse dynamics. We reinterpret PS from a dynamical perspective, showing that the standard PS update corresponds to a first-order discretization of the diffusion dynamics plus a residual correction capturing the mismatch between the denoised prediction and the data-consistent estimate. A second-order discretization, however, naturally introduces a temporal correction based on the variation of consecutive estimates. Building on this, we propose LAMP, combining the second-order update with the residual correction characterizing a PS technique. LAMP thus inherits a lagged temporal correction, and it can be implemented as a modular plug-in over the PS backbone. We show that LAMP preserves the structure of a posterior sampler, and we perform a one-step risk analysis to characterize when LAMP improves the reverse transition via a bias-variance trade-off. Experiments across multiple imaging tasks demonstrate consistent improvements over strong baselines such as DiffPIR and DDRM, without increasing the number of denoising evaluations.

### [11] [DistractMIA: Black-Box Membership Inference on Vision-Language Models via Semantic Distraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12574)
*Hongyi Tang,Zhihao Zhu,Yi Yang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出DistractMIA：一种仅基于输出、黑盒的视觉-语言模型（VLM）成员推断方法，通过向原图注入已知语义干扰并比较生成文本变化来判定成员身份；在多种VLM与基准上优于现有方法，并在医疗数据上同样有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VLM训练数据可能包含隐私/版权/敏感内容，需要成员推断进行审计。但已部署VLM常只能看到文本输出，现有方法依赖不可得的概率信号或基于遮挡/掩码、偏重物体中心假设，适用性受限。

Method: 提出DistractMIA：保留原图，注入预先设定的“语义干扰物”（distractor），不移除原有证据；在参考集上标定干扰配置；对同一输入进行多次生成，度量响应稳定性与对干扰的“跟随度”，据此计算成员分数；全程不访问logits/概率/隐状态，仅用输出文本。

Result: 在多种VLM与公开基准上，相比仅输出可用的方法和需要更强访问权限的基线，DistractMIA表现持续更优；在医疗基准上亦取得良好效果，显示其在非物体中心场景的适用性。

Conclusion: 语义干扰与多次生成稳定性可作为仅输出黑盒环境下可靠的成员信号；DistractMIA提升了VLM训练数据审计的可行性与泛化性，超越以往依赖概率或物体中心假设的方法。

Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) are trained on large-scale image-text corpora that may contain private, copyrighted, or otherwise sensitive data, motivating membership inference as a tool for training-data auditing. This is especially challenging for deployed VLMs, where auditors typically observe only generated textual responses. Existing VLM membership inference attacks either rely on probability-level signals unavailable in such settings, or use mask-based semantic prediction tasks whose effectiveness depends on object-centric visual assumptions. To address these limitations, we propose DistractMIA, an output-only black-box framework based on semantic distraction. Rather than removing visual evidence, DistractMIA preserves the original image, inserts a known semantic distractor, and measures how generated responses change. This design is motivated by the intuition that member samples remain more anchored to the original image semantics, while non-member samples are more easily redirected toward the distractor. To make this signal reliable, DistractMIA calibrates distractor configurations on a reference set and derives membership scores from repeated textual generations, capturing response stability and distractor uptake without accessing logits, probabilities, or hidden states. Experiments across multiple VLMs and benchmarks show that DistractMIA consistently outperforms both output-only and stronger-access baselines. Its performance on a medical benchmark further demonstrates applicability beyond object-centric natural images.

### [12] [3D Primitives are a Spatial Language for VLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12586)
*Junze Liu,Kun Qian,Florian Dubost,Kai Zhong,Arvind Srinivasan,Nan Chen,Anping Wang,Sam Zhang,Alejandro Mottini,Qingjun Cui,Tian Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文发现VLM能用可执行几何原语代码重建3D场景却在简单空间问答上失败，提出以“几何原语代码”作为空间理解中间表征，并通过新基准、推理策略与自监督微调，显著提升多数据集空间推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VLM在空间理解上呈现矛盾：能写出重建3D场景的代码（正确计数/类别/大致位置），却答不好同图像的基础空间问题。作者推断“几何原语+可执行代码”或是更稳定的空间表征与诊断工具，想量化不同语言差异并把这种能力迁移到一般视觉推理。

Method: 1) SpatialBabel基准：评测14个VLM在6种场景代码语言（编程/声明式3D原语）上的3D重建与QA，比较跨语言性能差异。2) Code-CoT：训练-free推理，把空间推理路线改为先生成原语场景代码再回答（代码链式思维）。3) S^3-FT：自监督空间微调，用模型自身的Three.js原语重建解析为结构化标注，无人类/教师，微调模型使原语空间知识迁移到通用视觉推理。

Result: - 同一模型在不同代码语言下的检测F1可相差至多5.7×；- Code-CoT使SpatialBabel-QA在原语场景上最高+6.4%，真实照片CV-Bench-3D上+5.0%；- 仅用原语图像训练，S^3-FT令Qwen3-VL-8B在SpatialBabel-Primitive-QA上+4.6~+8.6%，在CV-Bench-2D上+9.7%，在HallusionBench上+17%，并可迁移至其他模型家族。

Conclusion: 几何原语代码既是有效的空间诊断工具，也是可迁移的“空间词汇”。通过跨语言评测、代码化推理与自监督微调，可系统提升VLM的空间理解与泛化，且无需人工标注或教师模型；作者将发布所有资源。

Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) exhibit a striking paradox: they can generate executable code that reconstructs a 3D scene from geometric primitives with correct object counts, classes, and approximate positions, yet the same models fail at simpler spatial questions on the same image. We show that 3D geometric primitives (cubes, spheres, cylinders, expressed in executable code) serve as a powerful intermediate representation for spatial understanding, and exploit this through three contributions. First, we introduce \textbf{\textsc{SpatialBabel}}, a benchmark evaluating fourteen VLMs on primitive-based 3D scene reconstruction across six \emph{scene-code languages} (programming languages and declarative formats for 3D primitive scenes), revealing that a single model's object-detection F1 can vary by up to $5.7\times$ across languages. Second, we propose \textbf{Code-CoT} (Code Chain-of-Thought), a training-free inference strategy that routes spatial reasoning through primitive-based code generation. Code-CoT lifts the SpatialBabel-QA-Score by up to $+6.4$\% on primitive scenes and real-photo CV-Bench-3D accuracy by $+5.0$\% for VLMs with strong coding capabilities. Third, we propose \textbf{S$^{3}$-FT} (Self-Supervised Spatial Fine-Tuning), which self-supervisedly distills primitive spatial knowledge into general visual reasoning by parsing the model's own Three.js primitive-reconstructions into structured annotations and fine-tuning on the result, with \emph{no human labels and no teacher model}. Training on primitive images alone, S$^3$-FT improves Qwen3-VL-8B by $+4.6$ to $+8.6$\% on SpatialBabel-Primitive-QA, $+9.7$\% on CV-Bench-2D, and $+17$\% on HallusionBench; the recipe transfers across model families. These results establish geometric primitives in code as both a diagnostic and a transferable spatial vocabulary for VLMs. We will release all artifacts upon publication.

### [13] [TrackCraft3R: Repurposing Video Diffusion Transformers for Dense 3D Tracking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12587)
*Jisu Nam,Jahyeok Koo,Soowon Son,Jaewoo Jung,Honggyu An,Junhwa Hur,Seungryong Kim*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出TrackCraft3R：将预训练视频扩散Transformer（video DiT）重塑为单目视频的前馈致密3D跟踪器，单次前向即可输出以首帧为参考的全像素跨时跟踪点云与可见性；在多基准上达SOTA，且更快更省显存。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有致密3D跟踪要么基于从零训练的迭代式方法（多为合成数据），要么微调静态多视几何模型，均缺乏来自真实视频的大规模运动先验。与此同时，视频DiT蕴含互联网规模数据的时空先验，但其逐帧生成（frame-anchored）范式与参考锚定（reference-anchored）的跟踪需求不匹配，亟需桥接。

Method: 以视频DiT为基础，通过LoRA微调实现：1）双潜表示（dual-latent）：引入逐帧几何潜变量与参考锚定的轨迹潜变量作为密集查询，耦合已有的每帧重建点图（pointmap）；2）时间RoPE对齐：为每个轨迹潜变量显式编码目标时间戳；从而把DiT的逐帧生成范式转化为参考锚定的前馈致密跟踪。模型输入单目视频及其逐帧点图，一次前向直接输出首帧每像素在后续帧中的3D位置与可见性。

Result: 在标准稀疏与致密3D跟踪基准上取得SOTA；相比最强先验方法推理提速约1.3倍，峰值显存降低约4.6倍；对大位移与长序列表现稳健。

Conclusion: 通过双潜表示与时间RoPE对齐，将视频DiT从逐帧生成成功转化为参考锚定的前馈致密3D跟踪器。TrackCraft3R不仅性能领先，还具备更高效率与更强鲁棒性，显示以大规模视频先验赋能3D跟踪的有效路径。

Abstract: Dense 3D tracking from monocular video is fundamental to dynamic scene understanding. While recent 3D foundation models provide reliable per-frame geometry, recovering object motion in this geometry remains challenging and benefits from strong motion priors learned from real-world videos. Existing 3D trackers either follow iterative paradigms trained from scratch on synthetic data or fine-tune 3D reconstruction models learned from static multi-view images, both lacking real-world motion priors. Pre-trained video diffusion transformers (video DiTs) offer rich spatio-temporal priors from internet-scale videos, making them a promising foundation for 3D tracking. However, their frame-anchored formulation, which generates each frame's content, is fundamentally mismatched with reference-anchored dense 3D tracking, which must follow the same physical points from a reference frame across time. We present TrackCraft3R, the first method to repurpose a video DiT as a feed-forward dense 3D tracker. Given a monocular video and its frame-anchored reconstruction pointmap, TrackCraft3R predicts a reference-anchored tracking pointmap that follows every pixel of the first frame across time in a single forward pass, along with its visibility. We achieve this through two designs: (i) a dual-latent representation that uses per-frame geometry latents and reference-anchored track latents as dense queries, and (ii) temporal RoPE alignment, which specifies the target timestamp of each track latent. Together, these designs convert the per-frame generative paradigm of video DiTs into a reference-anchored tracking formulation with LoRA fine-tuning. TrackCraft3R achieves state-of-the-art performance on standard sparse and dense 3D tracking benchmarks, while running 1.3x faster and using 4.6x less peak memory than the strongest prior method. We further demonstrate robustness to large motions and long videos.

</details>

Abstract: Object detection in adverse weather is critical for the safety of autonomous vehicles; however, the scarcity of labelled, real-world foggy data remains a significant bottleneck. In this paper, we propose Clear2Fog (C2F), an end-to-end, physics-based pipeline that simulates fog on clear-weather datasets while ensuring sensor-level consistency across camera and LiDAR. By using monocular depth estimation and a novel atmospheric light estimation method, C2F overcomes structural artifacts and chromatic biases common in existing techniques. A human perceptual study confirms C2F's physical realism, with the generated images being preferred 92.95% of the time over an established method. Utilising a training set of 270,000 images from the Waymo Open Dataset, we conduct an extensive data efficiency study to investigate how environmental diversity influences model robustness. Our findings reveal that models trained on mixed-density fog datasets at 75% scale outperform those trained on fixed-density datasets at 100% scale. Furthermore, we investigate the sim-to-real transfer by fine-tuning pre-trained models on real-world foggy data. We demonstrate that a tenfold increase over the default fine-tuning learning rate successfully overcomes negative transfer from synthetic biases, resulting in a 1.67 mAP improvement over real-only baselines. The C2F pipeline provides a scalable framework for enhancing the reliability of autonomous systems in adverse weather and demonstrates the potential of diverse synthetic datasets for efficient model training.

### [15] [MambaPanoptic: A Vision Mamba-based Structured State Space Framework for Panoptic Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12640)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) MambaFPN：基于Mamba块的自顶向下特征金字塔，在各尺度以状态空间模型实现线性复杂度的全局一致表征；2) PanopticFCN式核生成器，统一生成things与stuff的卷积核用于无提议全景预测；3) 在多阶段加入QuadMamba特征精炼模块，进一步提升特征质量与全局一致性。

Abstract: Panoptic segmentation requires the simultaneous recognition of countable thing instances and amorphous stuff regions, placing joint demands on long-range context modelling, multi-scale feature representation, and efficient dense prediction. Existing convolutional and transformer-based methods struggle to satisfy all three requirements concurrently: convolutional architectures are limited in their capacity to model long-range dependencies, while transformer-based methods incur quadratic computational cost that is prohibitive at high resolutions. In this paper, we propose MambaPanoptic, a fully Mamba-based panoptic segmentation framework that addresses these limitations through two principal contributions. First, we introduce MambaFPN, a top-down feature pyramid that leverages Mamba blocks to generate globally coherent, multi-scale feature representations with linear computational complexity. Second, we adopt a PanopticFCN-style kernel generator that produces unified thing and stuff kernels for proposal-free panoptic prediction, enhanced by a QuadMamba-based feature refinement module applied at multiple network stages. Experiments on the Cityscapes and COCO panoptic segmentation benchmarks demonstrate that MambaPanoptic consistently outperforms PanopticDeepLab and PanopticFCN under comparable model sizes, and matches or surpasses Mask2Former on Cityscapes in PQ and AP while requiring fewer parameters.

### [16] [DIVER:Diving Deeper into Distilled Data via Expressive Semantic Recovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12649)
*Qianxin Xia,Zhiyong Shu,Wenbo Jiang,Jiawei Du,Jielei Wang,Guoming Lu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出DIVER：用预训练扩散模型对蒸馏数据进行“语义继承-引导-融合”两阶段（实为双阶段含三步）处理，去除架构特异噪声、恢复并巩固高层语义，从而显著提升跨架构泛化；在ImageNet 256上仅需约4GB显存、耗时与原始DiT相当。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单阶段数据蒸馏易学到与特定网络结构耦合的模式，导致跨架构迁移性能下降，且语义表达受抑、隐私与效率难兼顾。作者希望在保护隐私与高效训练的前提下，恢复与保留更通用、更可迁移的高层语义。

Method: 提出DIVER双阶段框架，利用预训练扩散模型：1) 语义继承：将“抽象蒸馏图像”的高层语义蒸馏到扩散模型的潜空间，过滤架构特异噪声、保留内在语义；2) 语义引导：在反向扩散过程中施加引导以增强原始语义的保持；3) 语义融合：仅在反向过程的具体化阶段提供引导，避免语义歧义和伪影，同时维持指导信息。输出为更可迁移的“不可读/非原始”代理数据。

Result: 在多种经典蒸馏技术上显著增益，跨架构泛化明显提升；在ImageNet 256×256 上处理时间与原始DiT相当，仅需约4GB显存。

Conclusion: 通过将扩散模型纳入数据蒸馏流程并分解为继承-引导-融合，DIVER有效恢复与巩固高层语义，缓解对特定架构的过拟合，实现高效、隐私友好的代理数据合成与更强的跨架构泛化。

Abstract: Dataset distillation aims to synthesize a compact proxy dataset that is unreadable or non-raw from the original dataset for privacy protection and highly efficient learning. However, previous approaches typically adopt a single-stage distillation paradigm, which suffers from learning specific patterns that overfit on a prior architecture, consequently suppressing the expression of semantics and leading to performance degradation across heterogeneous architectures. To address this issue, we propose a novel dual-stage distillation framework called ${\textbf{DIVER}}$, which leverages the pre-trained diffusion model to dive deeper into $\textbf{DI}$stilled data $\textbf{V}$ia $\textbf{E}$xpressive semantic $\textbf{R}$ecovery, an entire process of semantic inheritance, guidance, and fusion. Semantic inheritance distills high-level semantics of abstract distilled images into the latent space to filter out architecture-specific ``noise" and retain the intrinsic semantics. Furthermore, semantic guidance improves the preservation of the original semantics by directing the reverse procedure. Finally, semantic fusion is designed to provide semantic guidance only during the concrete phase of the reverse process, preventing semantic ambiguity and artifacts while maintaining the guidance information. Extensive experiments validate the effectiveness and efficiency of DIVER in improving classical distillation techniques and significantly improving cross-architecture generalization, requiring processing time comparable to raw DiT on ImageNet (256$\times$256) with only 4 GB of GPU memory usage. Code is available: https://github.com/einsteinxia/DIVER.

</details>


### [17] [CRAFT: Clinical Reward-Aligned Finetuning for Medical Image Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12650)
*Yunsung Chung,Alex El Darzi,Carlo El Khoury,Han Feng,Nassir Marrouche,Jihun Hamm*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出一种用于评估和提升医学图像生成临床一致性的框架：先定义“临床对齐分数”（CAS）作为四维度的对齐代理指标，再通过“临床奖励对齐微调”（CRAFT）将多模态大模型医学知识转移到扩散模型，显著降低幻觉式、临床不合理生成，并提升下游分类表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通用扩散模型在自然图像上很强，但适配医学影像时数据少、标注稀缺，易出现与病理不符的“幻觉式”生成。现有指标（如 FID、IS）无法度量单张图像与临床要点的一致性，因此需要一个能面向病理相关维度的评估指标与相应的对齐训练方法。

Method: 1) 提出 CAS：基于基础模型的代理评估，从视觉保真之外，以四个互补维度衡量生成图像的临床对齐度。2) 提出 CRAFT：以奖励为核心的适配框架，包含：a) 标签条件的提示增强；b) 临床核对清单；c) 可微的奖励优化；并将多模态 LLM 与视觉-语言模型中的医学知识迁移到扩散模型。3) 在四种不同医学成像模态上进行评测，与强基线比较。

Result: 在四个模态上，CRAFT 相较强基线提升 CAS 和下游分类性能；并将“低对齐尾部”低于真实图像参考阈值的占比进一步压低 5.5–34.7 个百分点，跨数据集平均相对降低 20.4%。还通过异构评估器、结构化清单审计、记忆化分析与医生盲测（CheXpert）等进行一致性验证。

Conclusion: CAS 为医学生成质量提供了更贴近临床的单样本对齐度量，CRAFT 则能利用多模态大模型知识与奖励优化，显著减少临床不合理与幻觉式生成，并带来下游任务收益，显示在医学影像适配中的有效性与稳健性。

Abstract: Foundation diffusion models can generate photorealistic natural images, but adapting them to medical imaging remains challenging. In medical adaptation, limited labeled data can exacerbate hallucination-like and clinically implausible synthesis, while existing metrics such as FID or Inception Score do not quantify per-image alignment with pathology-relevant criteria. We introduce the Clinical Alignment Score (CAS), a foundation-model-based proxy for clinical alignment that evaluates generated images along four complementary dimensions beyond visual fidelity. Building on CAS, we propose Clinical Reward-Aligned Finetuning (CRAFT), a reward-based adaptation framework that transfers medical knowledge from multimodal large language models and vision-language models through label-conditioned prompt enrichment, clinical checklists, and differentiable reward optimization. Across four diverse modalities, CRAFT improves CAS and downstream classification performance over strong adaptation baselines. Beyond average CAS gains, CRAFT reduces the empirical low-alignment tail below a real-image reference threshold by 5.5-34.7% points relative to the strongest baseline, corresponding to a 20.4% average relative reduction across datasets. These results indicate fewer hallucination-like generations under CAS, and are corroborated by out-of-family evaluator evaluation, structured checklist auditing, memorization analysis, and a blinded physician preference study on CheXpert.

</details>


### [18] [No One Knows the State of the Art in Geospatial Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12678)
*Isaac Corley,Nils Lehmann,Caleb Robinson,Gabriel Tseng,Anthony Fuller,Hamed Alemohammad,Evan Shelhamer,Jennifer Marcus,Hannah Kerner*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文审计GFMs领域发现评估与发布缺乏标准，导致无法公平比较与认定SOTA；提出六项社区规范以改善可复现性与可比性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GFMs被用于关键遥感任务，但现有文献在评测、协议、权重发布与预训练控制上不一致，致使研究者与用户无法判断哪种模型适配哪种任务与何者为SOTA。

Method: 对152篇GFM相关论文进行系统审计与对比：统计跨论文在相同模型/基准/协议下的性能分歧；梳理预训练数据配置的独特性；统计权重发布比例；并归纳问题成因与提出改进建议。

Result: 发现46处在同模同基准同协议下≥10分的性能冲突；可提取预训练数据的126篇中有94篇使用独一无二的配置；39%的论文未发布模型权重。

Conclusion: 当前问题源自社区协作失灵而非个别实验室；作者提出六项具体期望：1) 具名许可的权重发布；2) 共享核心评测集；3) 标注复用vs重跑基线；4) 报告方差；5) 统一评测框架；6) 将数据/架构/算法影响解耦的对照实验，以建立可比、可复现、可持续创新的GFM研究生态。

Abstract: Geospatial foundation models (GFMs) have been proposed as generalizable backbones for disaster response, land-cover mapping, food-security monitoring, and other high-stakes Earth-observation tasks. Yet the published work about these models does not give reviewers or users enough information to tell which model fits a given task. We argue that nobody knows what the current state of the art is in geospatial foundation models. The methods may be useful, but the GFM literature does not standardize evaluations, training and testing protocols, released weights, or pretraining controls well enough for anyone to compare or rank them. In a 152-paper audit, we find 46 cross-paper disagreements of at least 10 points for the same model, benchmark, and protocol; 94/126 papers with extractable pretraining data use a configuration no other paper uses; and 39% of GFM papers release no model weights. This lack of community standards can be solved. We propose six concrete expectations: named-license weight release, shared core evaluations, copied-versus-rerun baseline annotations, variance reporting, one shared evaluation harness, and data-vs-architecture-vs-algorithm controls. These gaps are a coordination failure, not a fault of any individual lab; the authors of this paper, like many others in the GFM community, have contributed to them. Rather than just critiquing the community, we aim to provide concrete steps toward a shared understanding of how to innovate GFMs.

### [19] [Visual Aesthetic Benchmark: Can Frontier Models Judge Beauty?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12684)
*Yichen Feng,Yuetai Li,Chunjiang Liu,Yuanyuan Chen,Fengqing Jiang,Yue Huang,Hang Hua,Zhengqing Yuan,Kaiyuan Zheng,Luyao Niu,Bhaskar Ramasubramanian,Basel Alomair,Xiangliang Zhang,Misha Sra,Zichen Chen,Radha Poovendran,Zhangchen Xu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该论文提出视觉审美评测应以“成组比较选择”而非单图打分进行，并构建VAB基准，显示当前MLLM在审美判断上与专家存在显著差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有审美评估多用单图标量分数，难以反映真实的相对偏好。作者通过受控实验发现：由分数导出的排序与专家直接两两比较不一致，且直接比较能获得更高一致性，于是动机是建立能捕捉比较信号的评测框架。

Method: 1) 进行八位专家的对照研究，对比分数排序与直接比较在一致性上的差异；2) 构建Visual Aesthetic Benchmark (VAB)：以相同题材的候选集做比较选择，覆盖美术、摄影、插画，共400个任务、1,195张图，每任务由10位独立专家给出共识标签（最佳/最差）；3) 在VAB上评测20个前沿MLLM与6个视觉质量奖励模型，并测试随机候选顺序的鲁棒性；4) 以2,000条专家示例微调35B模型，比较与397B开源权重模型的差距与可迁移性。

Result: 最强系统在三次随机候选顺序下同时正确选出最佳与最差图的任务准确率仅26.5%，远低于专家的68.9%；用2,000条专家数据微调的35B模型性能接近397B模型，表明比较信号可迁移、可提升。

Conclusion: 单图打分不足以刻画审美偏好；VAB提供首个以集合比较、专家标注为基础的审美评测平台，揭示并量化MLLM与专家审美间的显著差距，并为未来通过比较式训练与评测逐步缩小该差距提供路径。

Abstract: Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) are now routinely deployed for visual understanding, generation, and curation. A substantial fraction of these applications require an explicit aesthetic judgment. Most existing solutions reduce this judgment to predicting a scalar score for a single image. We first ask whether such scores faithfully capture comparative preference: in a controlled study with eight expert annotators, score-derived rankings align poorly with the same annotators' direct comparisons, while direct ranking yields substantially higher inter-annotator agreement on best- and worst-image labels. Motivated by this finding, we introduce the Visual Aesthetic Benchmark (VAB), which casts aesthetic evaluation as comparative selection over candidate sets with matched subject matter. VAB contains 400 tasks and 1,195 images across fine art, photography, and illustration, with labels derived from the consensus of 10 independent expert judges per task. Evaluating 20 frontier MLLMs and six dedicated visual-quality reward models, we find that the strongest system identifies both the best and the worst image correctly across three random permutations of the candidate order in only 26.5% of tasks, far below the 68.9% achieved by human experts. Fine-tuning a 35B-parameter model on 2,000 expert examples brings its accuracy close to that of a 397B-parameter open-weight model, suggesting that the comparative signal in VAB is transferable. Together, these results expose a clear and measurable gap between current multimodal models and expert aesthetic judgment, and VAB provides the first set-based, expert-grounded testbed on which that gap can be tracked and closed.

### [20] [MMCL-Bench: Multimodal Context Learning from Visual Rules, Procedures, and Evidence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12703)
*Yifan Chen,Fei Yin,Qingyan Bai,Zicheng Lin,Yujiu Yang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: MMCL-Bench提出针对多模态情境学习的基准，要求模型从视觉/混合模态的教学情境中学规则与流程并迁移到新样本。结果显示前沿模型在严格评测下解题率不到三分之一，暴露从证据定位到推理与作答全链路薄弱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准多聚焦文本情境学习或常规多模态问答，难以评估模型在真实视觉情境中“先找证据、再学规则、再应用”的能力缺口；需要系统性测量模型对任务本地规则、流程与经验模式的学习与迁移。

Method: 构建包含102个任务的基准，覆盖三类能力：规则体系应用、流程性任务执行、以及经验性发现与归纳。提供多种视觉与混合模态情境载体（图片、截图、手册、视频/帧序列），并采用严格的评分细则与诊断性消融/误差分析，分解评测链路：情境锚定、视觉证据抽取、情境推理、与响应构造。

Result: 在严格评分下，最强多模态模型也仅解决不到三分之一的任务。消融与误差分析显示，模型在全流程各环节均存在显著失败，包括无法可靠定位关键信息、提取视觉证据不充分、对学得的规则与流程推理薄弱、以及输出结构化回答不稳定。

Conclusion: MMCL-Bench揭示多模态情境学习是当前多模态模型的关键瓶颈；现有系统距离稳健学习并迁移任务本地规则与流程仍有明显差距，该基准可作为未来方法改进与诊断的参考平台。

Abstract: We introduce MMCL-Bench, a benchmark for multimodal context learning: learning task-local rules, procedures, and empirical patterns from visual or mixed-modality teaching context and applying them to new visual instances. Unlike text-only context learning or standard multimodal question answering, this setting requires models to recover and localize relevant evidence from images, screenshots, manuals, videos, and frame sequences before they can reason over the learned context. MMCL-Bench contains 102 tasks spanning three categories: rule system application, procedural task execution, and empirical discovery and induction. We evaluate frontier multimodal models with strict rubric-based scoring and find that current systems remain far from robust multimodal context learning, with even the strongest model solving fewer than one-third of tasks under strict evaluation. Diagnostic ablations and error analysis show that failures arise throughout the context-to-answer pipeline, including context anchoring, visual evidence extraction, context reasoning, and response construction. MMCL-Bench thus highlights multimodal context learning as an important unsolved capability bottleneck for current multimodal models.

### [21] [Inline Critic Steers Image Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12724)
*Weitai Kang,Xiaohang Zhan,Yizhou Wang,Mang Tik Chiu,Jason Kuen,Kangning Liu,Yan Yan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Inline Critic：在冻结的图像编辑模型的中间层内联地批判并引导隐表示，从而在一次前向传播中进行细粒度纠错，显著提升多项基准表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 图像编辑的难度在不同样本与同一图像的不同区域上高度异质；现有“事后”式改进（在整张图或一次去噪完成后才给出反馈）来得太晚，错过了在生成过程中及时校正的机会。作者好奇：能否在前向传播进行时就提供纠偏信号以节省迭代并更精准地聚焦错误区域？

Method: 先对冻结的图像编辑模型进行探测：发现生成能力主要出现在最后几层，但错误模式在早期层已基本确定（与最终错误图的秩相关0.83）。据此提出Inline Critic：在中间层插入可学习“批判”token，对模型中间预测进行评估并通过引导隐藏状态来即时修正。训练采用三阶段配方，从学习批判到稳定地驱动生成逐步过渡，并分析注意力与后续层预测被实质性影响。

Result: 在GEdit-Bench上达SOTA（7.89），在RISEBench相同骨干上+9.4分，在KRIS-Bench取得最强开源结果（81.92，超过GPT-4o）；可视化和统计显示critic改变了注意力分布与后续层更新。

Conclusion: 中间层错误模式可被早期识别并利用；通过内联批判token在前向过程中进行细粒度纠错，可稳定训练并显著提升编辑质量与区域对齐，优于事后式改进。

Abstract: Instruction-based image editing exhibits heterogeneous difficulty not only across cases but also across regions of an image, motivating refinement approaches that allocate correction to where the model struggles. Existing refinement signals arrive late, after a fully generated image or a completed denoising step. We ask whether such a signal can act within an ongoing forward pass. To investigate this, we probe a frozen image-editing model and find that although generation capability emerges only in the last few layers, the error pattern is already set in early layers (rank correlation \r{ho} = 0.83 with the final-layer error map). Based on this, we introduce Inline Critic, a learnable token that critiques a frozen model's predictions at its intermediate layers and steers its hidden states to refine generation during the forward pass. A three-stage recipe is proposed to stabilize the training from learning how to critique to steering generation. As a result, we achieve state of the art on GEdit-Bench (7.89), a +9.4 gain on RISEBench over the same backbone, and the strongest open-source result on KRIS-Bench (81.92, surpassing GPT-4o). We further provide analyses showing that the critic genuinely shapes the model's attention and prediction updates at subsequent layers.

</details>


### [22] [Is Video Anomaly Detection Misframed? Evidence from LLM-Based and Multi-Scene Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12725)
*Furkan Mumcu,Michael J. Jones,Anoop Cherian,Yasin Yilmaz*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 现有VAD研究追求跨场景通用“正常性”模型，提升了可扩展与泛化，但忽视了场景特异与情境相关的正常行为建模，导致语义偏置、定位能力受损，VAD被简化为动作识别。本文通过可视化与实证表明：真实应用多为单场景、需空间感知与可解释；应回归单场景、空间显式、可解释的建模以刻画环境内细粒度正常结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前方法依赖视频级弱监督与MLLM预训练特征，更倾向识别常见“异常类型”，而非偏离本场景正常模式，难以满足现实单场景VAD对局部几何、语义与活动模式的需求。作者希望纠正研究重心，强调与实际一致的建模范式。

Method: 提出对主流范式的再评估：设计针对性的可视化分析与实证实验，对多场景通用方法在单场景环境下的空间定位、语义偏置与错误归因进行对比评测，以揭示方法论局限。

Result: 实验与可视化显示，多场景通用+弱监督+MLLM特征的方案在单场景下存在显著语义偏置、空间定位能力弱，将检测简化为动作识别，难以捕捉细致的正常结构与异常偏离。

Conclusion: 要在实际VAD中取得有效进展，应转向单场景、空间感知且可解释的表述与训练策略，专注于刻画个体环境内的正常性细节结构，而非仅依赖跨场景通用表征与弱监督。

Abstract: Recent video anomaly detection research has expanded rapidly with an emphasis on general models of normality intended to work across many different scenes. While this focus has led to improvements in scalability and multi-scene generalization, it has also shifted the field away from modeling the scene-specific and context-dependent nature of normal behavior. Contemporary approaches frequently rely on video-level weak supervision and opaque pretrained representations from multi-modal large language models (MLLMs), which encourage models to respond to familiar semantic anomaly categories rather than to deviations from the normal patterns of a particular environment. This trend suppresses spatial localization, introduces semantic bias, and reduces anomaly detection to a form of action recognition. In this paper, we examine whether these prevailing formulations align with the core requirements of real-world VAD, which is typically performed within a single scene where normality is determined by local geometry, semantics, and activity patterns. Through targeted visual analyses and empirical evaluations, we demonstrate the practical consequences of these limitations and show that meaningful progress in VAD requires renewed focus on single-scene, spatially-aware, and explainable formulations that capture the nuanced structure of normality within individual environments.

### [23] [Just Ask for a Table: A Thirty-Token User Prompt Defeats Sponsored Recommendations in Twelve LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12772)
*Andreas Maier,Jeta Sopa,Gozde Gul Sahin,Paula Perez-Toro,Siming Bayer*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文复现并拓展了Wu等(2026)关于LLM在“软性赞助”提示下倾向推荐更贵赞助航班的发现，发现原结论总体可推广，但原文管线描述不足导致可重复性问题；同时提出一个30-token中立对比表用户提示可显著抑制赞助偏置（开源模型46.9%→1.0%，OpenAI模型53.0%→0%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验前沿LLM在隐性商业诱导下的行为是否稳健、是否可复现，并探索简单用户侧干预能否缓解偏置；同时评估评测流程与判别器（judge）对结果的敏感性。

Method: - 复现实验：对10个开源聊天模型+仍可用的2个专有模型（gpt-3.5-turbo, gpt-4o）运行与原文一致的评测任务，采用gpt-4o作为主判别器，并并行记录gpt-oss-120b与gpt-4o-mini标签作消融。
- 误差排查：对比文字管线与实现，定位3个“静默实现失误”对指标的影响。
- 统计检验：复估gpt-3.5-turbo的逻辑回归截距alpha，并在付费贷等有害产品情境下做200/200试验。
- 干预测试：加入一个约30 token的“请求中立对比表”用户提示，衡量赞助推荐率变化。

Result: - 可重复性：仅凭文字描述不足以复现；三个实现问题各自可让指标偏移数十百分点。
- 结论可推广：gpt-3.5-turbo的alpha=0.81，接近原文0.86；在财务困境用户场景，gpt-3.5-turbo与gpt-4o在200/200次中均推广发薪日贷款。
- 缓解有效性：中立对比表提示将赞助推荐率在开源模型均值从46.9%降至1.0%，在两款OpenAI模型从53.0%降至0%。
- 数据开源：提供原始数据、标签与脚本。

Conclusion: 原论文核心主张在更广模型集上成立，但评测管线需要精确、可执行的规范以保证复现性。极简的用户提示即可大幅降低赞助偏置，提示AI素养与比价门户等市场机制可作为宏观层面的缓解手段；但对有害产品的推荐问题仍未被这些机制完全约束。

Abstract: Wu et al. (2026) showed that most frontier large language models (LLMs) recommend a sponsored, roughly twice-as-expensive flight when their system prompt contains a soft sponsorship cue. We reproduce their evaluation on ten open-weight chat models plus the two of their twenty-three models that are still reachable today (gpt-3.5-turbo, gpt-4o). All reported rates in this paper are produced under the same judge the original paper used (gpt-4o); we additionally store every label under an open-weight (gpt-oss-120b) and a smaller proprietary (gpt-4o-mini) judge for an ablation. Three findings emerge. First, a prose description of an LLM evaluation pipeline is not, on its own, sufficient for accurate reproduction: we surfaced three silent implementation failures that each shifted a reported rate by tens of percentage points. Second, the central claims do generalise - the gpt-3.5-turbo logistic-regression intercept of alpha = 0.81 is within four points of the original alpha = 0.86, and 200 of 200 trials on gpt-3.5-turbo and gpt-4o promote a payday lender to a financially distressed user. Third, a thirty-token user prompt that asks the assistant for a neutral comparison table first cuts sponsored recommendation from 46.9% to 1.0% averaged across our ten open-source models, and from 53.0% to 0% averaged across the two OpenAI models. AI literacy and price-comparison portals are likely market-level mitigations; the harmful-product cell is bounded by neither. Raw data, labels and analysis scripts are at https://github.com/akmaier/Paper-LLM-Ads .

</details>

*Jianhao Zheng,Liyuan Zhu,Zihan Zhu,Iro Armeni*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: WildPose 提出一个统一的单目位姿估计框架，将前馈感知前端与可微分BA端到端优化相结合，在动态场景中稳健，同时在静态与低自运动数据集上保持SOTA表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有动态意识方法各自为政：基于语义的方法脆弱、按序列优化在短序列失效、学习模型在纯静态场景退化；需要一个在动态与静态皆鲁棒且统一的位姿估计框架。

Method: 以冻结的预训练 MASt3R 特征骨干为基础：1) 设计3D感知更新算子，融合前馈特征与可微分束调（BA）进行端到端优化；2) 构建高容量的运动掩码检测器，利用同一骨干的多层级3D感知特征辨识动态区域，从而在优化中抑制动态干扰。

Result: 在多基准上优于现有方法：动态（Wild-SLAM、Bonn）、静态（TUM、7-Scenes）和低自运动（Sintel）均取得一致性领先性能。

Abstract: Estimating camera pose in dynamic environments is a critical challenge, as most visual SLAM and SfM methods assume static scenes. While recent dynamic-aware methods exist, they are often not unified: semantic-based approaches are brittle, per-sequence optimization methods fail on short sequences, and other learned models may degrade on static-only scenes. We present WildPose, a unified monocular pose estimation framework that is robust in dynamic environments while maintaining state-of-the-art performance on static and low-ego-motion datasets. Our key insight is to connect two powerful paradigms in modern 3D vision: the rich perceptual frontend of feedforward models and the end-to-end optimization of differentiable bundle adjustment (BA). We achieve this with a 3D-aware update operator built on a frozen, pre-trained MASt3R feature backbone, together with a high-capacity motion mask detector that uses multi-level 3D-aware features from the same backbone. Extensive experiments show WildPose consistently outperforms prior methods across dynamic (Wild-SLAM, Bonn), static (TUM, 7-Scenes), and low-ego-motion (Sintel) benchmarks.

### [25] [FRAME: Forensic Routing and Adaptive Multi-path Evidence Fusion for Image Manipulation Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12826)
*Kaixiang Zhao,Tianrun Yu,Aoxu Zhang,Junhao Su,Porter Jenkins,Amanda Hughes*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出FRAME：一种将多种取证算法进行多路径路由与自适应证据融合的图像篡改检测框架，能按图像选择最有信息的取证路径并融合证据，以更稳健地检测与定位操作，跨多类篡改场景表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单一取证方法（无论手工特征还是深度模型）在鲁棒性、证据碎片化、跨篡改类型与成像条件的泛化方面受限；现有固定融合策略也难兼顾灵活性与可解释性。需要一种能组合多源取证证据、按图像自适应选择路径并保持可解释性的框架。

Method: 构建多路径取证分析空间，将多样取证算法作为候选路径；对每张输入图像，自适应选择最具信息量的取证路径（路由）；对各路径产出的互补证据进行融合，以提升检测与定位；同时保留来自多源证据的可解释线索。

Result: 在多种图像篡改情景下实验证明FRAME有效，较单方法或固定融合方案在检测与定位性能上更优。

Conclusion: 通过超越单一模型与固定融合，FRAME实现了更稳健、灵活、且可解释的图像取证推理；适用于多类篡改与条件变化。代码已开源。

Abstract: The proliferation of sophisticated image editing tools and generative artificial intelligence models has made verifying the authenticity of digital images increasingly challenging, with important implications for journalism, forensic analysis, and public trust. Although numerous forensic algorithms, ranging from handcrafted methods to deep learning-based detectors, have been developed for manipulation detection, individual methods often suffer from limited robustness, fragmented evidence, or weak generalization across manipulation types and image conditions. To address these limitations, we present \textbf{FRAME}, a method for \textbf{F}orensic \textbf{R}outing and \textbf{A}daptive \textbf{M}ulti-path \textbf{E}vidence fusion for image manipulation detection. FRAME organizes diverse forensic algorithms into a multi-path analysis space, adaptively selects informative forensic paths for each input image, and fuses complementary evidence to improve detection and localization performance. By moving beyond single-method analysis and fixed fusion strategies, FRAME provides a more robust and flexible approach to image forensic reasoning while preserving interpretable forensic cues from multiple evidence sources. Experimental results demonstrate the effectiveness of FRAME across diverse manipulation scenarios. Code is available at \href{https://github.com/kzhao5/FRAME}{https://github.com/kzhao5/FRAME}.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出PRISM：绕细胞核构建自适应同心围核区域，绕开精确细胞边界检测；在这些区域内融合颜色信息与基于灰度共生矩阵的纹理统计提取细胞质鲁棒描述；随后使用经校准的传统分类器堆叠集成进行判别。

Conclusion: 通过围核区代替显式细胞质边界与轻量传统模型的堆叠集成，可在异质染色与采集条件下实现鲁棒、可泛化的ALL细胞图像分析性能，减少对重型神经网络和大量标注的依赖。

Abstract: Automated analysis of peripheral blood smears for Acute Lymphoblastic Leukemia (ALL) is hindered by low contrast and substantial variability in cytoplasmic appearance, which complicate conventional membrane-based segmentation. We found that many recent approaches rely on heavy neural architectures and extensive training, but still struggle to generalize across staining and acquisition variability. To address these limitations, we propose the Perinuclear Ring-based Image Segmentation Method (PRISM), which replaces explicit cytoplasmic delineation with adaptive concentric zones constructed around the nucleus. These perinuclear regions enable the extraction of robust cytoplasmic descriptors by integrating color information with texture statistics derived from grey-level co-occurrence patterns, without requiring accurate cell-boundary detection. A calibrated stacking ensemble of traditional classifiers leverages these descriptors to achieve a high performance, with an accuracy of 98.46% and a precision-recall AUC of 0.9937.

### [28] [Prediction of Rectal Cancer Regrowth from Longitudinal Endoscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12855)
*Jorge Tapias Gomez,Despoina Kanata,Aneesh Rangnekar,Christina Lee,Hannah Williams,Hannah Thompson,J. Joshua Smith,Francisco Sanchez-Vega,Mert R. Sabuncu,Julio Garcia-Aguilar,Harini Veeraraghavan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出TREX：一种基于时间序列的深度学习方法，利用复诊内镜与复评内镜成对图像，通过Swin Transformer孪生网络与双重交叉注意力，无需配准即可判别完全/近完全缓解与局部再增生；在末次随访与提前3–12个月早期检测任务上优于基线，并达到与资深临床医师相当的判读准确度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: WW策略在直肠癌CR/近CR患者中可避免过度治疗，但随访中缺乏客观、早期、准确的局部再增生检测手段；传统影像学或人工阅片存在延迟与主观性，需要利用纵向信息的自动化模型提升早期发现能力。

Method: 构建TREX：以预训练Swin Transformer为骨干的孪生网络，分别提取复评（restaging）与随访内镜图像特征；通过双重交叉注意力融合两时点特征，无需空间配准；在两类训练设置下评估：（a）在末次随访判别LR vs CR；（b）在临床确认前3–6、6–12、12–24个月进行早期LR检测；并与Swin基线比较；同时以外科医生问卷进行临床验证，并探索将术前（pre-TNT）与复评图像组合预测治疗反应。

Result: 末次随访LR检测中，TREX达到敏感度97%±6%、平衡准确率90%±3%，优于所有Swin基线；在早期检测上，提前3–6个月与6–12个月的准确率分别为74%±1%、62%±4%，均超越基线；临床验证中总准确度与主治医师相当（TREX 86.21% vs 临床医师87.84%±1.28%）；预后/反应预测（pre-TNT+复评）平衡准确率73%±12%。

Conclusion: 利用纵向内镜图像的交叉注意力深度模型可在无配准条件下有效整合时序信息，提升WW随访中LR的检测与提前识别能力，表现接近资深临床医师，并对治疗反应预测具有潜力，提示其可用于改进直肠癌监测流程。

Abstract: Clinical trial studies indicate benefit of watch-and-wait (WW) surveillance for patients with rectal cancer showing a complete or near clinical response (CR) directly after treatment (restaging). However, there are no objectively accurate methods to early detect local tumor regrowth (LR) in patients undergoing WW from follow-up exams. Hence, we developed Temporal Rectal Endoscopy Cross-attention (TREX), a longitudinal deep learning approach that combines pairs of images acquired at restaging and follow-up to distinguish CR from LR. TREX uses pretrained Swin Transformers in a siamese setting to extract features from longitudinal images and dual cross-attention to combine the features without spatial co-registration between image pairs. TREX and Swin-based baselines were trained under two settings: (a) detecting LR or CR at the last available follow-up and (b) early detection of LR at 3--6, 6--12, and 12--24 months before clinical confirmation. TREX achieved the highest accuracy in detecting LR with a high sensitivity of 97% $\pm$ 6% and a balanced accuracy of 90% $\pm$ 3%, and outperformed all baselines in early detection at both 3--6 (74% $\pm$ 1%) and 6--12 months (62% $\pm$ 4%) prior to clinical detection. Clinical validation via a surgeon survey showed that TREX matched attending-level overall accuracy (TREX: 86.21% vs.\ Clinicians: 87.84% $\pm$ 1.28%). Finally, we explored TREX's ability to predict treatment response by combining pre-treatment (pre-TNT) and restaging endoscopies, achieving a balanced accuracy of 73% $\pm$ 12%. These results show that longitudinal deep learning analysis of endoscopy may improve surveillance and enable earlier identification of rectal cancer regrowth.

### [29] [Adaptive Conformal Prediction for Reliable and Explainable Medical Image Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12917)
*One Octadion,Novanto Yudistira,Lailil Muflikhah*

TL;DR: 提出一种改进RAPS的自适应Lambda准则，优化最差分层覆盖，缓解医学影像分类中不确定样本的过度自信与分层欠覆盖，同时保持小预测集规模并具备跨域泛化。

Method: 在RAPS框架中引入自适应Lambda准则，最小化按预测集规模分层后的最坏覆盖违例；在OrganAMNIST上训练评估，并进行跨域验证至PathMNIST；结合定量Grad-CAM分析以解释多标签预测与注意力区域的关系。

Conclusion: 该自适应Lambda准则提升了CP在医学影像中的可靠性，控制最差分层覆盖而不显著牺牲效率，适用于安全关键医疗AI场景，并在跨域数据上具备稳健性。

Abstract: Deep learning models for medical imaging often exhibit overconfidence, creating safety risks in ambiguous diagnostic scenarios. While Conformal Prediction (CP) provides distribution-free statistical guarantees, standard methods such as Regularized Adaptive Prediction Sets (RAPS) optimize for average efficiency and can mask severe failures on difficult inputs.
  We propose an Adaptive Lambda Criterion for RAPS that minimizes the worst-case coverage violation across prediction set size strata. On OrganAMNIST (58,850 abdominal CT images, 11 classes), standard size-optimized RAPS converges to near-deterministic behavior with stratified undercoverage on uncertain samples, while our method achieves 95.72 percent global coverage with average set size 1.09 and at least 90 percent coverage across all strata. Cross-domain validation on PathMNIST (107,180 pathology images, 9 classes) confirms generalizability.
  Quantitative Grad-CAM analysis (rho = -0.30, p < 1e-22) shows that multi-label predictions correspond to focused attention on anatomically ambiguous regions. These results demonstrate that the proposed method improves reliability while maintaining efficiency, making it suitable for safety-critical medical AI applications.

### [30] [GuardMarkGS: Unified Ownership Tracing and Edit Deterrence for 3D Gaussian Splatting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12919)
*Utae Jeong,Jaewan Choi,Junseok Lee,Jongheon Jeong,Sang Ho Yoon,ByoungSoo Koh,Sangpil Kim*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出首个面向3D Gaussian Splatting(3DGS)的统一版权保护框架，同时实现可追溯水印与对指令驱动编辑的对抗性阻断，在保证画面质量下提高位准确率与编辑阻遏效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 3DGS已广泛用于新视角合成，但公开后资产易被他人无授权使用与被指令式3D编辑工具任意篡改。现有方法要么只做水印追责、无法阻止编辑，要么只做对抗性阻断、无法证明所有权，缺乏兼顾的统一方案。

Method: 在所有高斯上联合优化两支路目标：1) 场景级水印目标保证可恢复的所有权位；2) 对抗性编辑阻遏目标，通过三种干预组合——潜变量锚点分离(latent-anchor separation)、去噪轨迹偏离(denoising-trajectory diversion)、跨注意力偏离(cross-attention diversion)——来把编辑过程引向失败或无关方向。并提出基于更新显著性的高斯选择策略，对掩码选中的关键高斯赋予更强对抗更新，以在水印可恢复性、编辑阻遏与渲染保真之间取得更好平衡。

Result: 在Mip-NeRF 360与Instruct-NeRF2NeRF场景上实验表明，该框架在位准确率、编辑阻遏强度与渲染质量三方面实现更优权衡，相较单一水印或单一对抗方法更稳健。

Conclusion: 将所有权追踪与未授权编辑阻遏统一为单一优化框架，可更有效地为3DGS资产提供实用的版权保护，并在不显著牺牲渲染保真的前提下实现可验证与可阻断的双重防护。

Abstract: 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) is becoming a practical representation for novel view synthesis, but its growing adoption, together with rapid advances in instruction-driven 3DGS editing, also exposes a dual copyright risk: once a 3DGS-based asset is released, it can be used without permission and manipulated through 3D editing. Existing protection methods address only one side of this problem. Watermarking can trace ownership after unauthorized use, but it cannot prevent malicious editing. Adversarial edit-deterrence methods can disrupt editing, but they do not provide evidence of ownership. To the best of our knowledge, we present the first unified protection framework for 3DGS that jointly optimizes ownership tracing and unauthorized editing deterrence. Our framework combines a scene-wide watermarking objective over all Gaussians with an adversarial objective for edit deterrence. The adversarial branch combines latent-anchor separation, denoising-trajectory diversion, and cross-attention diversion to divert the editing trajectory, while an update-saliency-motivated Gaussian selection strategy assigns stronger adversarial updates to mask-selected Gaussians, improving the balance among watermark recovery, edit deterrence, and rendering fidelity. Experiments on scenes from Mip-NeRF 360 and Instruct-NeRF2NeRF demonstrate that the proposed framework achieves a favorable balance among bit accuracy, edit deterrence, and rendering quality. These results suggest that practical copyright protection of 3DGS-based assets can be more effectively addressed by integrating ownership tracing and unauthorized editing deterrence into a single optimization framework.

### [31] [Anatomy-Slot: Unsupervised Anatomical Factorization for Homologous Bilateral Reasoning in Retinal Diagnosis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12929)
*Yingzhe Ma,Xiao Yang,Yuguo Yin,Zheyu Wang*

TL;DR: 提出Anatomy-Slot：在双眼视网膜成对输入上，通过无监督解剖槽(slot)对齐与跨注意力，实现结构对应，AUC相对匹配ViT-L提升4.2%，并在噪声与配对打乱实验中验证依赖与鲁棒性；还在REFUGE进行视盘定量定位与注意力可解释性分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临床上视网膜诊断常依赖双眼同源解剖结构的比较（如视盘不对称），但主流深度模型多为单眼输入，无法显式建模双眼对应关系，可能限制性能与可解释性。

Method: 提出Anatomy-Slot：将图像patch token无监督分解为若干“解剖槽”，通过双向跨注意力在左右眼之间对齐槽，实现结构级瓶颈与对应约束；在ODIR-5K上与匹配的ViT-L做对比；进行配对打乱试验与高斯噪声压力测试检验对应依赖与抗扰动；在REFUGE上进行视盘定位量化与跨注意力定位分析。

Result: 在ODIR-5K上（n=10随机种子），AUC较ViT-L提升4.2%，给出95%置信区间，Wilcoxon符号秩检验W=0, p=0.002，显著优于基线；配对打乱导致性能下降，表明模型依赖结构对应；在噪声下保持较好鲁棒性；在REFUGE上视盘定位与注意力可视化显示较好解剖对准。

Conclusion: 显式的双眼解剖对应建模能提升视网膜疾病诊断性能与可解释性；基于无监督槽对齐的Anatomy-Slot为双眼结构对比提供通用框架，并在多项实验中展现统计显著的优势与鲁棒性。

Abstract: Retinal diagnosis is inherently bilateral: clinicians compare homologous structures across eyes (e.g., optic disc asymmetry), yet most deep models operate on monocular representations. We investigate whether explicit structural correspondence improves diagnosis, and propose Anatomy-Slot to operationalize this hypothesis. Anatomy-Slot introduces an unsupervised anatomical bottleneck by decomposing patch tokens into slots and aligning slots across eyes via bidirectional cross-attention. On ODIR-5K with $n=10$ seeds, the method improves AUC by 4.2% over a matched ViT-L baseline (95% CIs; Wilcoxon signed-rank test, $W=0$, $p=0.002$). Pairing disruption and stress testing under Gaussian noise provide controlled tests of correspondence dependence and robustness under corruption. We further report quantitative optic disc grounding on REFUGE and cross-attention localization analysis.

### [33] [CRePE: Curved Ray Expectation Positional Encoding for Unified-Camera-Controlled Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12938)
*Seonghyun Jin,Youngmin Kim,Sunwoo Park,Jong Chul Ye*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出CRePE：一种面向统一相机模型（UCM，含广角/鱼眼）的曲线射线期望位置编码，用于提升相机可控视频生成中的几何稳健性与控制稳定性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出CRePE：将每个图像token表示为其源射线上的深度感知“位置分布”（曲线射线路径的期望），显式建模广角/鱼眼导致的投影路径几何；通过在冻结的Video DiT中加入几何注意力适配器（Geometric Attention Adapter），把逐token的场景距离信息注入选定的注意力层；并使用单目几何基础模型提供的伪监督稳定训练。此外，提出Radial MixForcing，将同一位置编码通道扩展为外部径向图（radial-map）控制，用于场景几何条件生成与源视频运动迁移。

Result: 在多项几何与感知质量指标上提升，同时视频质量指标保持有竞争力；对比RayRoPE风格端点位置编码基线，CRePE在受控消融中取得更优的平均排序，显示UCM感知的投影路径集成在多种相机模型下更有效；并能实现超出相机控制之外的外部几何/运动迁移控制。

Conclusion: CRePE提供了与UCM兼容、对广角/鱼眼稳健的曲线射线期望位置编码，通过几何注意力适配与伪监督实现稳定相机控制与更好的几何一致性，并可统一拓展到外部径向几何控制与运动迁移。

Abstract: Camera-conditioned video generation requires positional encoding that remains reliable under changes in camera motion, lens configuration, and scene structure. However, existing attention-level camera encodings either provide ray-only camera signals or rely on pinhole camera geometry, limiting their applicability to general camera control under the Unified Camera Model, including wide-angle and fisheye lenses. To address this limitation, we propose Curved Ray Expectation Positional Encoding (CRePE). CRePE represents each image token as a depth-aware positional distribution along its source ray, providing a Unified Camera Model-compatible positional encoding that captures the projected-path geometry induced by wide-angle and fisheye cameras. CRePE is implemented through a Geometric Attention Adapter added to frozen video DiTs, injecting token-wise scene-distance information into selected attention layers and stabilizing it with pseudo supervision from a monocular geometry foundation model. This design leads to more stable camera control and improves several geometry-aware and perceptual-quality metrics, while remaining competitive on video-quality metrics. Controlled positional-encoding ablations show a better overall average rank than a RayRoPE-style endpoint PE baseline, demonstrating the effectiveness of UCM-aware projected-path integration across diverse camera models. Furthermore, by extending the same positional-encoding pathway to external geometry control through Radial MixForcing, CRePE supports external radial-map control for scene-geometry-conditioned generation and source-video motion transfer beyond camera control.

### [34] [DirectTryOn: One-Step Virtual Try-On via Straightened Conditional Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12939)
*Xianbing Sun,Jiahui Zhan,Liqing Zhang,Jianfu Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出针对VTON任务的一步生成方案，通过让条件采样轨迹更“直”，在效率与质量上达SOTA。核心做法：纯条件传输、服装保真损失、自一致性损失，并配合一步蒸馏，实现高质量、低延迟试穿。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散/流式VTON依赖多步采样，推理昂贵；现有加速忽视VTON强条件约束这一结构特性。预训练基模与条件生成不匹配，导致采样轨迹弯曲，限制一步生成潜力。

Method: 1) 纯条件传输：去除无关噪声驱动，强化由条件(人物与服装)主导的生成路径；2) 服装保真(保留)损失：约束生成保留输入服装外观细节与几何；3) 自一致性损失：在不同条件扰动/视角下保持输出一致，促直化轨迹；4) 一步蒸馏：将多步教师的行为蒸馏到一步学生模型，实现单步采样。

Result: 在广泛实验中，一步采样下达到与或优于现有方法的SOTA视觉质量与试穿保真，同时显著降低推理成本与延迟。

Conclusion: VTON输出受条件强约束，适合“直线式”采样；通过针对性损失与一步蒸馏，可在单步下实现高效高质的试穿生成，为高效VTON设定新基准。

Abstract: Recent diffusion- and flow-based VTON methods achieve strong results with pretrained generative models, but their reliance on multi-step sampling incurs high inference cost, while existing acceleration methods largely overlook the intrinsic structure of the try-on task. In this paper, we highlight a key observation: VTON outputs are highly constrained by the conditional inputs, suggesting that the conditional sampling trajectory can be much straighter than that in general image generation, making one-step generation a natural solution. However, limited task-specific data makes training from scratch impractical, forcing existing methods to fine-tune pretrained models whose objectives do not encourage such straight conditional trajectories. Thus, the deviation from an ideal straight path mainly comes from the mismatch between pretrained base models and the conditional nature of try-on generation, rather than from the task itself. Motivated by this insight, we encourage straighter VTON sampling trajectories through three targeted modifications: pure conditional transport, a garment preservation loss, and a self consistency loss. We further introduce a one-step distillation stage. Extensive experiments show that our method achieves state-of-the-art performance with one-step sampling, establishing a new standard for efficient and high-quality VTON.

### [35] [Debunking Grad-ECLIP: A Comprehensive Study on Its Incorrectness and Fundamental Principles for Model Interpretation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12952)
*Yongjin Cui,Xiaohui Fan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文指出：Grad-ECLIP的“中间特征”解释路径并不新颖，且与注意力路径等价；作者给出Attention-ECLIP作为计算更简的等价实现，并通过推导与实验证明等价性。同时，论文批评Grad-ECLIP的解释并非源模型的真实解释，且与模型性能不一致，进而提出两条解释应遵循的基本原则以避免此类错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前Transformer解释方法分为注意力权重为主与梯度/中间特征为主两路。Grad-ECLIP代表后一类并在ICML 2024提出，被视为新范式。作者动机：1) 澄清“中间特征路径”的新颖性与与注意力路径的关系；2) 检验Grad-ECLIP的有效性与忠实性；3) 给出更简洁、可验证的等价实现并总结可靠解释的基本原则。

Method: - 理论：在现有注意力解释框架上构造Attention-ECLIP，并对Grad-ECLIP进行形式化推导，证明两者在假设条件下等价（中间特征导向=注意力导向的重参数化）。- 实证：在多数据集/任务上比较Grad-ECLIP与Attention-ECLIP的解释图、重要性分布与指标，对齐度与稳定性评估；检验解释与模型性能的相关性与因果干预一致性。- 误差分析：定位Grad-ECLIP导致失真的环节（如梯度通过中间态的投影/归一化、非线性截断、未保持原模型前向路径等），并提炼两条原则。

Result: - 证明了Grad-ECLIP与注意力路径的等价性；Attention-ECLIP在计算上更简单、稳定。- 发现Grad-ECLIP生成的热力图/重要性与原模型决策不一致，且与性能指标失配；在对齐与因果遮挡测试中显著劣于等价的注意力实现。

Conclusion: 中间特征驱动的Grad-ECLIP并非新技术路线，而是注意力路线的等价变体；其实现存在方法学缺陷，导致解释偏离原模型与性能失配。作者据此强调两条基本原则：解释应忠于原模型的前向与参数（faithfulness），解释度量应与模型性能和因果干预一致（consistency/causality）。

Abstract: Grad-ECLIP is published at ICML 2024 and represents a new Transformer interpretation technical route (intermediate features-based). First, this paper demonstrates that the intermediate features-based technical route is not a novel one. Based on the existing attention-based route, we have developed Attention-ECLIP, which is completely equivalent to Grad-ECLIP but with simpler computation. Both through formal derivation and experimental validation, we prove that the intermediate feature-based route represented by Grad-ECLIP is actually an equivalent variant of the attention-based route. Next, this paper demonstrates that the Grad-ECLIP method is flawed. The model interpretation results obtained by Grad-ECLIP are not those of the original model, and the interpretation results are misaligned with the model's performance. We analyze the causes of Grad-ECLIP's flaws and propose, or rather, explicitly emphasize two fundamental principles that model interpretation should adhere to in order to avoid similar errors.

### [36] [Seg-Agent: Test-Time Multimodal Reasoning for Training-Free Language-Guided Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12953)
*Chao Hao,Jun Xu,Ji Du,Shuo Ye,Ziyue Qiao,Xiaodong Cun,Guangcong Wang,Xubin Zheng,Zitong Yu*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Language-guided segmentation transcends the scope limitations of traditional semantic segmentation, enabling models to segment arbitrary target regions based on natural language instructions. Existing approaches typically adopt a two-stage framework: employing Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) to interpret instructions and generate visual prompts, followed by foundational segmentation models (e.g., SAM) to produce masks. However, due to the limited spatial grounding capabilities of off-the-shelf MLLMs, these methods often rely on extensive training on large-scale datasets to achieve satisfactory accuracy. While recent advances have introduced reasoning mechanisms to improve performance, they predominantly operate within the textual domain, performing chain-of-thought reasoning solely based on abstract text representations without direct visual feedback. In this paper, we propose Seg-Agent, a completely training-free framework that pioneers Explicit Multimodal Chain-of-Reasoning. Unlike prior text-only reasoning, our approach constructs an interactive visual reasoning loop comprising three stages: generation, selection, and refinement. Specifically, we leverage Set-of-Mark (SoM) visual prompting to render candidate regions directly onto the image, allowing the MLLM to ``see'' and iteratively reason about spatial relationships in the visual domain rather than just the textual one. This explicit multimodal interaction enables Seg-Agent to achieve performance comparable to state-of-the-art training-based methods without any parameter updates. Furthermore, to comprehensively evaluate generalization across diverse scenarios, we introduce Various-LangSeg, a novel benchmark covering explicit semantic, generic object, and reasoning-guided segmentation tasks. Extensive experiments demonstrate the effectiveness and robustness of our method.

### [37] [AdaFocus: Adaptive Relevance-Diversity Sampling with Zero-Cache Look-back for Efficient Long Video Understanding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12954)
*Xiao Yang,Yingzhe Ma,Haoxuan Yu,Zixin Li,Ning Qin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: AdaFocus 将长视频理解从“一次性编码”转为“循序取证”。先用查询感知的自适应相关-多样采样生成紧凑预览，再在模型不确定时按需回溯，从磁盘零缓存取回高分辨率证据，兼顾覆盖、细节与效率。实验证明在多基准上更高效更准确，显著降低视觉token并免预缓存。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长视频方法要么密集编码，内存与时延代价高；要么稀疏抽帧，细节丢失且不可逆，难以兼顾时间覆盖、视觉细节与计算效率。需要一种既高效又可在需要时恢复细节的范式。

Method: 提出 AdaFocus，包括两部分：1) AdaRD 采样器：查询感知、兼顾相关性与多样性，若查询缺乏局部锚点则切换到全局聚类，生成信息量高的“视频预览”；2) 不确定性触发的精炼：非一次性缓存帧，而是在模型置信度不足时“按需回看”，通过零缓存 I/O 直接从磁盘取回高分辨率帧，避免预加载的开销，将被丢弃的细节转化为可按需恢复的证据。

Result: 在7个长视频基准上，较强基线取得更好的效率-准确率折中；相较单次密集编码推理，在 VideoMME 上+2.59 准确率、在 Charades-STA 上+8.39 mIoU，同时视觉token消耗约降33倍，并通过零缓存检索无需内存中预缓存帧。

Conclusion: 将“渐进式预览”与“零缓存按需精炼”结合，是可扩展多媒体推理的有效范式；可在不牺牲覆盖与细节的前提下显著提升效率与性能。

Abstract: Long video understanding is heavily bottlenecked by a rigid one-shot paradigm: existing methods either densely encode videos at prohibitive memory and latency costs, or aggressively compress them into sparse frame sets that irreversibly discard fine-grained evidence needed for downstream reasoning. Consequently, current models struggle to simultaneously balance temporal coverage, visual details, and computational efficiency.
  We propose AdaFocus, an efficient framework that rethinks long-video understanding as progressive evidence acquisition rather than one-pass encoding. AdaFocus relies on two tightly coupled components. First, a Query-Aware Adaptive Relevance-Diversity sampler (AdaRD) produces a compact yet informative video preview, adaptively switching to global clustering when the query lacks reliable local grounding. Second, instead of caching exhaustive frame sequences in memory, AdaFocus introduces an uncertainty-triggered refinement mechanism. It performs targeted look-back only when the model is not confident, retrieving high-resolution evidence directly from disk via a zero-cache I/O design. This turns discarded visual details from an irreversible loss into on-demand recoverable evidence without paying the cost of exhaustive preloading.
  Experiments on seven standard long-video benchmarks show that AdaFocus delivers a substantially better efficiency-accuracy trade-off than strong baselines. Compared with conventional dense encoding, AdaFocus achieves improved task performance (e.g., +2.59 accuracy on VideoMME, +8.39 mIoU on Charades-STA over single-pass inference) while reducing visual token consumption by ~33x and eliminating the need for in-memory frame pre-caching through its zero-cache disk retrieval design. These findings suggest that progressive preview combined with zero-cache evidence refinement is a highly effective paradigm for scalable multimedia reasoning.
